	function setIsCurated () {
		$('#news-feed').attr('data-curated', espn_ui.isCurated);
		$(document).trigger('checkIfShouldAutoUpdate');
		espn_ui.checkIfShouldAutoUpdate = true;
	}

	if (document.readyState == 'complete') {
		setIsCurated();
	} else {
		window.onload = setIsCurated;
	}
